7:00pm\nShow 8:00pm\n\n\nMs. Lauryn Hill to bring the ‘Small Axe’ performance series to Flyway At Fox Grand Opening on Friday, June 26 \n\nLimited tickets available starting June 18 @ 12pm PST\n\n(Pomona, CA) Flyway At Fox (the new rooftop venue at the legendary Fox Theater Pomona) will be hosting a Grand Opening featuring Ms. Lauryn Hill on Friday, June 26. A limited quantity of tickets will be available for purchase on Thursday, June 18.\n\nFirst known as a prestigious movie house in the 1930’s, the Fox Theater Pomona is now – as the LA Times would put it – one of “the top 30 southern California concert spots.” The famed venue has been attracting artists, celebrities, and attendees from all over the globe to their 2,000 capacity hall. Now, at their sister venue Flyway At Fox, they are attracting the same level of prestige, but to an intimate 300 capacity hall.\n\nFlyway At Fox serves as the only rooftop live event space in the hidden gem that is Pomona Arts Colony. Ornately decorated in an art-deco Vaudeville style, Flyway At Fox is the common ground between some of southern California’s major cities (being 30 miles east of Los Angeles, 30 miles west of San Bernardino, and 20 miles north of Orange County).\n\nSince its Soft Opening in September 2014, Flyway At Fox has hosted an array of artists – soon to join this roster of talent will be the legendary singer/rapper/songwriter Ms. Lauryn Hill. Following a string of intimate east coast performances in prominent venues such as The Howard in Washington DC and Highline Ballroom in New York, Ms. Lauryn Hill will bring her ‘Small Axe’ performance series exclusively to the Grand Opening of Flyway At Fox on Friday, June 26. A limited amount of tickets will be available for purchase starting June 18, 2015 at 12pm PST on www.eventbrite.com.
